<hr>
<a name="1257"/>
<h1>指令</h1>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td><b>创建时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-9-1 9:29</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>更新时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-9-1 15:52</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>作者：</b></td><td><i>李洪岩</i></td></tr>
</table>
</div>
<br/>

<div>
<span><div>对于指令，可以把它简单的理解成在特定DOM元素上运行的函数，指令可以扩展这个元素的功能。</div><div><br/></div><div>ng-copy:复制绑定的内容时，触发绑定的函数或者表达式</div><div><br/></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(245, 245, 245);"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px; color: inherit; copied:?{{copied}}</span></code></div><div><br/></div><div>ng-cloak</div><div>ng-cloak 指令用于AnjularJS应用在加载时，防止AnjularJS代码未加载完成而出现的问题，即显示AnjularJS代码</div><div><span style="border: 0px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; style="color:#c3e887;">&quot;b&quot;</span><span style="color:#6dc2b8;">&gt;<br/></span><span style="color:#6dc2b8;">? ? ? ? ? ? &lt;</span><span style="color:#ff5370;">input?</span><span style="color:#ffcb6b;">type=</span><span style="color:#c3e887;">&quot;text&quot;?</span><span style="color:#ffcb6b;">value=</span><span style="color:#c3e887;">&quot;CCC&quot;?</span><span 119, 0);"><br/></span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><font face="courier new">ng-transclude</font></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span 16px;">ng-value指令用于设置input和select元素的value属性。</span></font>&lt;input&gt; 和 &lt;select&gt; 元素支持该属性。</div><div style="border: 1px solid rgb(212, 212, 212); margin: 0px; padding: 5px; width: 715.781px; 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><font face="courier new"><span style="font-size: 16px;">expression用于设置ng-value的值</span></font></div></div><div><span <a name="1259"/>
<h1>AngularJS 表单验证</h1>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td><b>创建时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-9-1 14:29</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>更新时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-9-1 15:48</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>作者：</b></td><td><i>李洪岩</i></td></tr>
</table>
</div>
<br/>

<div>
<span><div><span style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><b><span style="font-size: 32px;">常用的表单验证指令?</span></b></span></div><div style="margin: 15px auto 2px; padding: 0px; display: block; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 2px 10px; font-size: 16px; font-weight: bold; display: block; font-family: 'Microsoft Yahei'; color: white; box-shadow: rgb(95, 90, 75) 0px 0px 0px 1px, rgba(10, 10, 0, 0.498039) 1px 1px 6px 1px; border-top-left-radius: 4px; border-top-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-left-radius: 4px; text-shadow: rgb(34, 34, 34) 2px 2px 3px; clear: both; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(43, 102, 149); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><div>1. 必填项验证</div></div></div><div><p style="margin: 10px auto; padding: 0px; text-indent: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.92px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">某个表单输入是否已填写，只要在输入字段元素上添加HTML5标记required即可：</p><div style="margin: 5px 0px; padding: 8px; border-width: 2px 2px 2px 5px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(176, 216, 255); overflow: auto; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;, 微软雅黑, Consolas, Arial, 宋体; font-size: 12px !important; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot; !important; font-size: 12px !important;">&lt;input?type=&quot;text&quot;?required?/&gt;?<br/></div></div></div><div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 2px 10px; font-size: 16px; font-weight: bold; display: block; font-family: 'Microsoft Yahei'; color: white; box-shadow: rgb(95, 90, 75) 0px 0px 0px 1px, rgba(10, 10, 0, 0.498039) 1px 1px 6px 1px; border-top-left-radius: 4px; border-top-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-left-radius: 4px; text-shadow: rgb(34, 34, 34) 2px 2px 3px; clear: both; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(43, 102, 149); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><div>2. 最小长度</div></div><div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div style="margin: 10px auto; padding: 0px; text-indent: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>验证表单输入的文本长度是否大于某个最小值，在输入字段上使用指令ng-minleng= &quot;number&quot;：</div></div><div style="margin: 5px 0px; padding: 8px; border-width: 2px 2px 2px 5px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(176, 216, 255); overflow: auto; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;, 微软雅黑, Consolas, Arial, 宋体; font-size: 12px !important; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot; !important; font-size: 12px !important;">&lt;input?type=&quot;text&quot;?ng-minlength=&quot;5&quot;?/&gt;?<br/></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 2px 10px; font-size: 16px; font-weight: bold; display: block; font-family: 'Microsoft Yahei'; color: white; box-shadow: rgb(95, 90, 75) 0px 0px 0px 1px, rgba(10, 10, 0, 0.498039) 1px 1px 6px 1px; border-top-left-radius: 4px; border-top-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-left-radius: 4px; text-shadow: rgb(34, 34, 34) 2px 2px 3px; clear: both; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(43, 102, 149); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><div>3. 最大长度</div></div><div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div style="margin: 10px auto; padding: 0px; text-indent: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>验证表单输入的文本长度是否小于或等于某个最大值，在输入字段上使用指令ng-maxlength=&quot;number&quot;：</div></div><div style="margin: 5px 0px; padding: 8px; border-width: 2px 2px 2px 5px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(176, 216, 255); overflow: auto; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;, 微软雅黑, Consolas, Arial, 宋体; font-size: 12px !important; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot; !important; font-size: 12px !important;">&lt;input?type=&quot;text&quot;?ng-maxlength=&quot;20&quot;?/&gt;<br/></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 2px 10px; font-size: 16px; font-weight: bold; display: block; font-family: 'Microsoft Yahei'; color: white; box-shadow: rgb(95, 90, 75) 0px 0px 0px 1px, rgba(10, 10, 0, 0.498039) 1px 1px 6px 1px; border-top-left-radius: 4px; border-top-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-left-radius: 4px; text-shadow: rgb(34, 34, 34) 2px 2px 3px; clear: both; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(43, 102, 149); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><div>4. 模式匹配</div></div><div><p style="margin: 10px auto; padding: 0px; text-indent: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.92px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">使用ng-pattern=&quot;/PATTERN/&quot;来确保输入能够匹配指定的正则表达式：</p><div style="margin: 5px 0px; padding: 8px; border-width: 2px 2px 2px 5px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(176, 216, 255); overflow: auto; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;, 微软雅黑, Consolas, Arial, 宋体; font-size: 12px !important; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot; !important; font-size: 12px !important;">&lt;input?type=&quot;text&quot;?ng-pattern=&quot;/[a-zA-Z]/&quot;?/&gt;?<br/></div></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 2px 10px; font-size: 16px; font-weight: bold; display: block; font-family: 'Microsoft Yahei'; color: white; box-shadow: rgb(95, 90, 75) 0px 0px 0px 1px, rgba(10, 10, 0, 0.498039) 1px 1px 6px 1px; border-top-left-radius: 4px; border-top-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-left-radius: 4px; text-shadow: rgb(34, 34, 34) 2px 2px 3px; clear: both; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(43, 102, 149); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><div><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体;">5. 电子邮件</span></div></div><div><p style="margin: 10px auto; padding: 0px; text-indent: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.92px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">验证输入内容是否是电子邮件，只要像下面这样将input的类型设置为email即可：</p><div style="margin: 5px 0px; padding: 8px; border-width: 2px 2px 2px 5px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(240, 240, 255) rgb(176, 216, 255); overflow: auto; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;, 微软雅黑, Consolas, Arial, 宋体; font-size: 12px !important; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot; !important; font-size: 12px !important;">&lt;input?type=&quot;email&quot; /&gt;?<br/></div></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 2px 10px; font-size: 16px; display: block; box-shadow: rgb(95, 90, 75) 0px 0px 0px 1px, rgba(10, 10, 0, 0.498039) 1px 1px 6px 1px; border-top-left-radius: 4px; border-top-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-right-radius: 4px; border-bottom-left-radius: 4px; text-shadow: rgb(34, 34, 34) 2px 2px 3px; clear: both; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(43, 102, 149); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><div><b><span style="font-family: 'Microsoft Yahei';"><span style="color: white;">6. 数字</span></span></b></div></div><div><p style="margin: 10px auto; padding: 0px; text-indent: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.92px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">$parsers的值是一个由函数组成的数组，当用户同控制器进行交互，并且ngModelController中的<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: underline;"><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 153);"><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">$setViewValue()</strong></span></em></span>方法被调用时，其中的函数在当用户同控制器进行交互，并且ngModelController中的$setViewValue()方法被调会以流水线的形式被逐一调用。ngModel从DOM中读取的值会被<em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 153);"><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">传入$parsers</strong></span></em>中的函数，并依次被其中的解析器处理。这是为了对值进行处理和修饰。</span></div><div><span style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br/></span></div></div></div><div><h3 style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 2px 10px; font-size: 16px; font-weight: bold; display: block; font-family: &quot;Microsoft Yahei&quot;; color: white; box-shadow: rgb(95, 90, 75) 0px 0px 0px 1px, rgba(10, 10, 0, 0.498039) 1px 1px 6px 1px; border-radius: 4px; text-shadow: rgb(34, 34, 34) 2px 2px 3px; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background: rgb(43, 102, 149);"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">$formatters</span></h3><div style="margin: 10px auto; padding: 0px; text-indent: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>$formatters的值是一个由函数组成的数组，其中的函数会以流水线的形式在数据模型的值发生变化时被逐一调用。它和$parser流水线互不影响，用来对值进行格式化和转换，以便在绑定了这个值的控件中显示。</div><div><br/></div></div><h3 style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 2px 10px; font-size: 16px; font-weight: bold; display: block; font-family: &quot;Microsoft Yahei&quot;; color: white; box-shadow: rgb(95, 90, 75) 0px 0px 0px 1px, rgba(10, 10, 0, 0.498039) 1px 1px 6px 1px; border-radius: 4px; text-shadow: rgb(34, 34, 34) 2px 2px 3px; clear: both; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background: rgb(43, 102, 149);">?$viewChangeListeners</h3><div style="margin: 10px auto; padding: 0px; text-indent: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>$viewChangeListeners的值是一个由函数组成的数组，其中的函数会以流水线的形式在视图中的值发生变化时被逐一调用。通过$viewChangeListeners，可以在无需使用$watch的情况下实现类似的行为。由于返回值会被忽略，因此这些函数不需要返回值。</div></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></div><div><hr/></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></div><div><a href="http://www.cnblogs.com/rohelm/p/4033513.html">http://www.cnblogs.com/rohelm/p/4033513.html</a></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: 'Courier New';"><br/></span></span></div><div><span </div>

<a name="1255"/>
<h1>核心原理</h1>

<span><div><span style="font-size: 32px;">Anjularjs启动过程</span></div><div><br/></div><div>步骤一：</div><div>? ? ?用自执行函数的形式让整个代码在加载完成之后立即执行</div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 10px; margin: 0px 0px 10px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 225); border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(249, 249, 247);"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px; color: inherit; border-radius: 0px; background-color: transparent;">(function(window,?document,?undefined)</code></div><div>? ? ?在window上暴露一个唯一的全局对象：anjular</div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 10px; margin: 0px 0px 10px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 225); border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(249, 249, 247);"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px; color: inherit; border-radius: 0px; background-color: transparent;">? ?//如果window.angular已经有值了，就把原有的赋值给前面angular，如果没有则用window.angular空对象赋值给angular</code><div><span style="color: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">angular?=?window.angular?||?(window.angular?=?{}),</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: inherit;"><span style="background-color: transparent;"><span style="font-size: inherit;">angularModule,</span></span></span></div><div><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px; color: inherit; border-radius: 0px; background-color: transparent;">uid?=?0;</code></div></div><div>? <a name="1202"/>
<h1>AnjularJS中的依赖注入</h1>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td><b>创建时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 11:07</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>更新时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-31 19:07</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>作者：</b></td><td><i>李洪岩</i></td></tr>
</table>
</div>
<br/>

<div>
<span><div>?????AnjularJS中与依赖注入相关的有anjular.module()、anjular.injector()、$injector、$provide。在anjularjs中，anjular.module()、$provide相当于服务的注册；anjular.injector()、$injector用来获取对象（anjularjs会自动完成依赖注入）。</div><div><br/></div><div><hr/></div><div><br/></div><div>? ? ?AnjularJS中依赖关系的声明主要有三种方式：</div><ul><li>? ? ?anjular.module()既可以创建新的模块，也可以获取已有的模块，是创建还是获取，由参数个数决定。</li></ul><div style="margin-left:40px;">? ? ? <span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, '‘Courier New‘', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: nowrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">angular</span><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, '‘Courier New‘', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: nowrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">.</span><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, '‘Courier New‘', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: nowrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">module</span><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, '‘Courier New‘', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: nowrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">(</span><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, '‘Courier New‘', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: nowrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">name</span><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, '‘Courier New‘', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: nowrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">,</span><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, '‘Courier New‘', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: nowrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">?</span><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, '‘Courier New‘', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: nowrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">[</span><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, '‘Courier New‘', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: nowrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">requires</span><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, '‘Courier New‘', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: nowrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">],</span><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, '‘Courier New‘', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: nowrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">?</span><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, '‘Courier New‘', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: nowrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">[</span><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, '‘Courier New‘', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: nowrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">configFn</span><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, '‘Courier New‘', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: nowrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">]);</span></div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; padding: 0px; white-space: nowrap;">? ? ? ? ? ?????name：字符串类型，代表模块的名称；</span></span></span></span></div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; padding: 0px; white-space: nowrap;">? ? ? ? ? ?????requires：字符串的数组，代表该模块依赖的其他模块列表，如果不依赖其他模块，用空数组即可；</span></span></span></span></div><div style="padding: 0px; text-decoration: none; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin-left:40px;"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, 'Courier New', monospace; padding: 0px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; padding: 0px; white-space: nowrap;">? ? ? ? ? ?????configFn：用来对该模块进行一些配置。</span></span></span></span></div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63); font-family: '‘Helvetica Neue‘', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">? ? ? ? ?? angular.Module中提供了这5个服务注册方法:constant()、value()、factory()、service()、provide()</span></div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><span style="font-family: '‘Helvetica Neue‘', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);"><br/></span></span></span></div><ul><li><span style="font-family: '‘Helvetica Neue‘', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);">? ? ? ? ?</span> $provide提供了provide()、constant()、value()、factory()、service()来创建各种不同性质的服务</span></li></ul><div><span style="font-family: '‘Helvetica Neue‘', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><br/></span></span></div><ul><li><span style="font-family: '‘Helvetica Neue‘', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">? ? ? ? ? anjular.injector()</span></span></li></ul><div><span style="font-family: '‘Helvetica Neue‘', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ?anjular.injector()方法可以获取到注入器，但是没有和模块绑定，这种做法是没有意义的，相当于创建了一个空的注入器，正确的做法是：在</span></span></div><div><span style="font-family: '‘Helvetica Neue‘', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">? ? ? ? ? ? ?? ?????创</span></span><span style="font-family: '‘Helvetica Neue‘', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">建注入器的时候指定加载的模块，使加载的模块的方法注入到注入器中。</span></span></div><div><span style="font-family: '‘Helvetica Neue‘', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><br/></span></span></div><div style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; padding: 5px; border: 1px dotted rgb(170, 170, 170); table-layout: fixed; color: rgb(63, 63, 63); font-size: 12px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(246, 246, 246);">var?myModule?=?angular.module('myModule',?[]);<br/>
myModule.service('myService',?function()?{<br/>
? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? this.my?=?0;<br/>
});<br/></div><div><span style="font-family: '‘Helvetica Neue‘', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><br/></span></span></div><div style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; padding: 5px; border: 1px dotted rgb(170, 170, 170); table-layout: fixed; color: rgb(63, 63, 63); font-size: 12px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(246, 246, 246);">var?herModule?=?angular.module('herModule',?[]);<br/>
herModule.service('herService',?function()?{<br/>
? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? this.her?=?1;<br/>
});<br/></div><div><span style="font-family: '‘Helvetica Neue‘', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><br/></span></span></div><div style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; padding: 5px; border: 1px dotted rgb(170, 170, 170); table-layout: fixed; color: rgb(63, 63, 63); font-size: 12px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(246, 246, 246);">var?injector?=?angular.injector([&quot;myModule&quot;,&quot;herModule&quot;]);<br/>
alert(injector.get(&quot;myService&quot;).my);<br/>
alert(injector.get(&quot;herService&quot;).her);<br/></div><div><span style="font-family: '‘Helvetica Neue‘', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><br/></span></span></div><div><br/></div><div><hr/></div><div><br/></div><div><span style="font-family: '‘Helvetica Neue‘', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">AnjularJS中三种获取依赖的方式：</span></span>?推断型<span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63); font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 18px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; display: inline !important; float: none; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">、声明性、内联型</span></div><div style="padding: 5px; border: 1px dotted rgb(170, 170, 170); table-layout: fixed; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(246, 246, 246);"><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);"><br/></span></span></span></div><div><font color="#3F3F3F">推断型注入</font></div><div><font color="#3F3F3F">var myModule = anjular.module('myModule',[]);</font></div><div><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);">var myFun = function($scope){</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);">? ? ?$scope.name = &quot;aaa&quot;;<br/></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);">}</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);">myModule.controller('myController',myFun);</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: Arial;"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);"><br/></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: Arial;"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);"><br/></span></span></span></div><div>声明型注入</div><div>var myModule = anjular.module('myModule',[]);</div><div>var myFun = function(myParam){</div><div>? ? ?myParam.name = &quot;aaa&quot;;</div><div>}</div><div>myFun.$inject = ['$socpe'];</div><div>myModule.controller('myContro',myFun);</div><div><br/></div><div>内联型注入</div><div>var myModule = angular.module('myModule',[]);</div><div>myModule.controller('myContro',['$scope',function($scope){</div><div>? ? ?$scope.name = &quot;aaa&quot;;</div><div>}]);</div><div><span style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);"><br/></span></span></span></div></div></div></span>

<a name="1192"/>
<h1>AngularJs $http 请求服务 - 野兽' - 博客园</h1>

<div>
<span><div style="-evernote-webclip:true"><br/></div><div style="background-color: rgb(230, 230, 230);"><div style="box-shadow:rgba(100, 100, 100, 0.298039) 0px 2px 6px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="text-align:left;"><div style="text-overflow:ellipsis;overflow:hidden;"><div style="text-overflow:ellipsis;overflow:hidden;"><div><h1 style="float:left;margin:0px;padding:0px;border-left:3px solid rgb(33, 117, 155);margin-bottom:10px;clear:both;font-weight:bold;font-size:130%;width:100%;border:0px;padding-left:5px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><a href="http://www.cnblogs.com/ys-ys/p/4984639.html" style="margin:0px;padding:0px;outline:none;text-decoration:none;color:rgb(33, 117, 155);transition:all 0.4s linear 0s;">AngularJs $http 请求服务</a></span></h1></div><div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><div style="margin:0px;padding:0px;margin-bottom:20px;word-break:break-word;"><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-size:18px;">$http</span></strong></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">$http是Angular的一个核心服务，它有利于浏览器通过XMLHttpRequest 对象或者 JSONP和远程HTTP服务器交互。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">$HTTP API 是基于 $q服务暴露的deferred/promise APIs。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">快捷使用方式：</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">$http.get</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">$http.head</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">$http.post</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">$http.put</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">$http.delete</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">$http.jsonp</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">$http.patch</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">设置HTTP请求头：</strong></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">$HTTP服务将会给所有请求自动创建HTTP头。这个默认设置能完全的通过访问$httpProvider.defaults.headers配置对象配置。目前包含默认配置：</span></span></p><div style="border:1px solid rgb(204, 204, 204);padding:5px;overflow:auto;margin:5px 0px;color:rgb(0, 0, 0);background-color:rgb(245, 245, 245);font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;"><pre style="margin:0px;padding:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">  $httpProvider.defaults.headers.common
        </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">//</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">-- Accept:application/json,text/plain</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">  $httpProvider.defaults.headers.post
        </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">//</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">-- Content-Type:application/json</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">  $httpProvider.defaults.headers.put
        </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">//</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">-- Content-Type:application/json</span></pre></div><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">添加或覆盖这些默认值</strong></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">添加或删除这些配置对象的属性。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">全局配置</strong>：</span></span></p><div style="border:1px solid rgb(204, 204, 204);padding:5px;overflow:auto;margin:5px 0px;color:rgb(0, 0, 0);background-color:rgb(245, 245, 245);font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;"><pre style="margin:0px;padding:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;">
  $httpProvider.defaults.headers.post = {“my-header”:”value”}
</pre></div><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">单请求配置</strong>：</span></span></p><div style="border:1px solid rgb(204, 204, 204);padding:5px;overflow:auto;margin:5px 0px;color:rgb(0, 0, 0);background-color:rgb(245, 245, 245);font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;"><div style="margin:0px;padding:0px;margin-top:5px;background-color:rgb(245, 245, 245);"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;padding-right:5px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;"><a href="#" style="margin:0px;padding:0px;outline:none;color:black;text-decoration:underline;border:none;background-color:rgb(245, 245, 245);" title="复制代码"><img src="anjularjs_files/copycode.gif" type="image/gif" alt="复制代码" height="20" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 700px; border: none; background-color: rgb(245, 245, 245); height: auto;" width="20"/></a></span></div><pre style="margin:0px;padding:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">  $http({

  $http.defaults.cache = <span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">true</span>/false;

  .config([“$httpProvider”,</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">function</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">($httpProvider){
    $httpProvider.interceptors.push(“yourInterceptors”);
  }])
  .factory(“yourInterceptors”,[“$q”,”dependency”, </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">function</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">($q,dependency){
    </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">return</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;"> {
      “request”:</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">function</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">(config){
        </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">//</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;"> do something on success</span>
        <span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">return</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;"> config;
      }，
    “requestError”:</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">function</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">(rejection){
       </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">//</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;"> do something on error</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">       If(canRecover(rejection)){
        </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">return</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;"> responseOrNewPromise
       }
       </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">return</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;"> $q.reject(rejection);
      },
    “response”:</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">function</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">(response){
       </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">//</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;"> do something on success</span>
       <span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">return</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;"> response;
      },
    “responseError”:</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">function</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">(rejection){
       </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">//</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;"> do something on error</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">       If(canRecover(rejection)){
         </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">return</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;"> responseOrNewPromise
       }
      </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">return</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;"> $q.reject(rejection);
      }
   };
  }]);</span></pre><div style="margin:0px;padding:0px;margin-top:5px;background-color:rgb(245, 245, 245);"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;padding-right:5px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;"><a href="#" style="margin:0px;padding:0px;outline:none;color:black;text-decoration:underline;border:none;background-color:rgb(245, 245, 245);" title="复制代码"><img src="anjularjs_files/copycode [5].gif" type="image/gif" alt="复制代码" height="20" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 700px; border: none; background-color: rgb(245, 245, 245); height: auto;" width="20"/></a></span></div></div><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">依赖</strong>：$httpBackend $cacheFactory $rootScope $q $injector</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">使用</strong>：$http(config);</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">参数</strong>：</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">method</strong></em>：字符串，请求方法。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">url</strong></em>：字符串，请求地址。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">params</strong></em>：字符串或者对象，将使用paramserializer序列化并且作为GET请求的参数。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">data</strong></em>：字符串或者对象，作为请求信息数据的数据。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">headers</strong></em>：对象，字符串或者函数返回表示发送到服务器的HTTP请求头。如果函数的返回值为空，则headers则不发送。函数接受一个配置对象作为参数。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">xsrfHeaderName</em></strong>：字符串，填充XSRF令牌的HTTP请求头名称。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">xsrfCookieName</strong></em>：字符串，含有XSRF令牌cookie的名字。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">transformRequest</strong></em>：函数/函数的数组。转换函数或者一个包含转换函数的数组。转换函数获取http请求体和请求头，并且返回他们的转换版（通常是序列化）。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">transformResponse</strong></em>：函数/函数的数组。转换函数或者一个包含转换函数的数组。转换函数获取http响应体和响应头，并且返回他们的转换版（通常是序列化）。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">paramSerializer</strong></em>：字符串或者返回字符串的函数。用于编写请求参数（指定为对象）的字符串表示形式的函数。如果指令是字符串，那么将被解释为通过$injector注册的函数，这意味着你能通过注册服务方式创建你自己的序列化程序。默认的序列化是$httpParamSerializer；或者你可以使用$httpParamSerializerJQLike。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">cache</strong></em>：boolean，如果为true，一个默认的$http缓存将被作为请求的缓存，否则如果存在一个用$cacheFactory创建的缓存实例，则将用于缓存。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">timeout</strong></em>：数值，毫秒，超时则让请求中止。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">withCredentials</strong></em>：boolean，是否设置withcredentials flag的XHR对象。查看更多信息的凭据。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">responseType</strong></em>：字符串，响应头类型。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">返回</strong>：</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">data</strong></em>：字符串或对象。变换函数变换后的响应体。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">status</strong></em>：数值，响应的http状态码。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">headers</strong></em>：函数，响应头的getter函数。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">config</strong></em>：对象，用于生成请求的配置对象。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">statusText</strong></em>：字符串，响应的HTTP状态文本。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">方法</strong>：</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">get(url,[config]);</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">url：请求地址。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">config：请求配置对象。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">delete(url,[donfig]);</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">url：请求地址。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">config：请求配置对象。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">head(url,[config]);</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">url：请求地址。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">config：请求配置对象。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">jsonp(url,[config]);</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">url：请求地址。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">config：请求配置对象。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">post(url,data,[config]);</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span
