style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">data：请求内容。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">config：请求配置对象。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">put(url,data,[config]);</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">url：请求地址。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">data：请求内容。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">config：请求配置对象。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">patch(url,data,[config]);</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">url：请求地址。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">data：请求内容。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">config：请求配置对象。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">属性</strong>：</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">pendingRequests</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">当前正在等待的请求的配置对象数组。主要是为了用于调试目的。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;">defaults??</strong></em></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">请求头配置默认属性。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-size:18px;">$httpParamSerializerJQLike</span></strong></span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">Http参数序列化程序。序列化程序也将按字母顺序排序的参数。</span></span></p><p style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">使用代码：</span></span></p><div style="border:1px solid rgb(204, 204, 204);padding:5px;overflow:auto;margin:5px 0px;color:rgb(0, 0, 0);background-color:rgb(245, 245, 245);font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;"><div style="margin:0px;padding:0px;margin-top:5px;background-color:rgb(245, 245, 245);"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;padding-right:5px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;"><a href="#" style="margin:0px;padding:0px;outline:none;color:black;text-decoration:underline;border:none;background-color:rgb(245, 245, 245);" title="复制代码"><img src="anjularjs_files/copycode [6].gif" type="image/gif" alt="复制代码" height="20" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 700px; border: none; background-color: rgb(245, 245, 245); height: auto;" width="20"/></a></span></div><pre style="margin:0px;padding:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;">
  (<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">function</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;"> () {
    angular.module(</span>&quot;Demo&quot;<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">, [])
    .controller(</span>&quot;testCtrl&quot;,[&quot;$http&quot;, &quot;$httpParamSerializerJQLike&quot;<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">,testCtrl]);
    </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">function</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;"> testCtrl($http, $httpParamSerializerJQLike){
      </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">var</span> data = { id: 1, value: &quot;hello&quot; };<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">//
</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">      $http({
          method: </span>&quot;post&quot;<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">,
          data: data,</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">//</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">Form Data = {&quot;id&quot;:1,&quot;value&quot;:&quot;hello&quot;}</span>
          url: &quot;/url&quot;<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">,
          headers: { </span>&quot;Content-Type&quot;: &quot;application/x-www-form-urlencoded&quot;<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;"> },
          success: </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">function</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;"> (d) { console.log(d); }
      });
      $http({
          method: </span>&quot;post&quot;<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">,
          data: $httpParamSerializerJQLike(data),</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">//</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#008000;">Form Data 变成 id:1  value:hello</span>
          url: &quot;/url&quot;<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;">,
          headers: { </span>&quot;Content-Type&quot;: &quot;application/x-www-form-urlencoded&quot;<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;"> },
          success: </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#0000ff;">function</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;color:#000000;"> (d) { console.log(d); }
      });
    };
  }());</span></pre><div style="margin:0px;padding:0px;margin-top:5px;background-color:rgb(245, 245, 245);"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;padding-right:5px;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;font-size:12px;"><a href="#" style="margin:0px;padding:0px;outline:none;color:black;text-decoration:underline;border:none;background-color:rgb(245, 245, 245);" title="复制代码"><img src="anjularjs_files/copycode [7].gif" type="image/gif" alt="复制代码" height="20" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 700px; border: none; background-color: rgb(245, 245, 245); height: auto;" width="20"/></a></span></div></div><div style="padding:0px;margin:10px auto;text-indent:0px;"><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif;">请求除了$http，还有$resource，关于后者，后面再提，先说明下$http，在最后例子的2个$http请求的时候，还加了headers设置&quot;Content-Type&quot;: &quot;application/x-www-form-urlencoded&quot;，这是因为有些小伙伴提出请求没有Form Data，只有 Request Payload，那么当我们设置请求头的Content-Type值为application/x-www-form-urlencoded时，就能看见Form Data了。实测可行...</span></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></span>
</div>
<hr>
<a name="1181"/>
<h1>AngularJs 服务</h1>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td><b>创建时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-29 18:54</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>更新时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 10:55</i></td></tr>
</table>
</div>
<br/>

<div>
<span><div style="-evernote-webclip:true"><br/></div><div style="box-shadow:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0980392) 0px 4px 10px;background:white;box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgb(254, 254, 254);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 5px; font-family: inherit; font-weight: normal; color: inherit; text-rendering: optimizelegibility; font-size: 24px;"><div>走进AngularJs(六) 服务</div></div><div style="padding-bottom: 5px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: dashed; border-bottom-color: rgb(211, 211, 211); font-size: 14px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px;"><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><br/></span></div></div></div><div style="padding: 20px 5px 25px; margin-bottom: 0px; overflow-x: hidden; word-wrap: break-word; word-break: break-all; min-height: 340px;"><div style="font-size:16px;"><h2 style="margin:0px 0px 0.5em;font-family:inherit;color:inherit;text-rendering:optimizeLegibility;font-weight:bold;font-size:18px;text-indent:1em;">一、认识服务（service）</h2><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">服务这个概念其实并不陌生，在其他语言中如java便有这样的概念，其作用就是对外提供某个特定的功能，如消息服务，文件压缩服务等，是一个独立的模块。ng的服务是这样定义的：</span></span></p><blockquote style="padding:0px 0px 0px 15px;margin:0px 0px 1.5em;border-left:5px solid rgb(10, 162, 132);padding-left:10px;font-size:14px;background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);word-wrap:break-word;word-break:break-all;"><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;margin-bottom:0px;font-weight:inherit;font-style:italic;font-size:16px;text-indent:0px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">Angular services are singletons objects or functions that carry out specific tasks common to web apps.</span></span></p></blockquote><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">它是一个单例对象或函数，对外提供特定的功能。</span></span></p><ul style="padding:0px;margin:0px 0px 0.75em 25px;list-style-type:none;padding-left:0px;font-size:16px;"><li style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">首先是一个单例，即无论这个服务被注入到任何地方，对象始终只有一个实例。</span></span></li><li style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">其次这与我们自己定义一个function然后在其他地方调用不同，因为服务被定义在一个模块中，所以其使用范围是可以被我们管理的。ng的避免全局变量污染意识非常强。</span></span></li></ul><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">ng提供了很多内置的服务，可以到API中查看</span> <a href="http://docs.angularjs.org/api/" rel="nofollow" style="transition:0.25s;outline:none 0px;color:rgb(148, 148, 148);text-decoration:none;border-bottom:1px dashed rgb(148, 148, 148);font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">http://docs.angularjs.org/api/</a> <span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">。知道了概念，我们来拉一个service出来溜溜，看看到底是个什么用法。（从这篇文章开始，我就使用jsfiddle来写示例代码了，再也不折腾博客园的变态编辑器了~）</span></span></p><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">我们在controller中直接声明$location服务，这依靠ng的依赖注入机制。$location提供地址栏相关的服务，我们在此只是简单的获取当前的地址。</span></span></p><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">服务的使用是如此简单，我们可以把服务注入到controller、指令或者是其他服务中。</span></span></p><h2 style="margin:0px 0px 0.5em;font-family:inherit;color:inherit;text-rendering:optimizeLegibility;font-weight:bold;font-size:18px;text-indent:1em;">二、自定义服务</h2><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">如同指令一样，系统内置的服务以$开头，我们也可以自己定义一个服务。定义服务的方式有如下几种：</span></span></p><ul style="padding:0px;margin:0px 0px 0.75em 25px;list-style-type:none;padding-left:0px;font-size:16px;"><li style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">使用系统内置的$provide服务</span></span></li><li style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">使用Module的factory方法</span></span></li><li style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">使用Module的service方法</span></span></li></ul><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">下面通过一个小例子来分别试验一下。我们定义一个名为remoteData服务，它可以从远程获取数据，这也是我们在程序中经常使用的功能。不过我这里没有远程服务器，就写死一点数据模拟一下。</span></span></p></div><div style="font-size:16px;"><div style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;"><div><span style="color:#008000;"><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;">//</span></span><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;"><span style="color:#008000;">使用$provide来定义</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">var</span></span>?app?=?angular.module(<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'MyApp'</span>,?[],?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">function</span></span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">($provide)?{</span></div><span style="color:#000000;">? ? $provide.factory(</span><span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'remoteData'</span>,?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">function</span></span><span style="color:#000000;">()?{<br/>
? ? ? ?</span> <span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">var</span></span>?data?=?{name:<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'n'</span>,value:<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'v'</span><span style="color:#000000;">};<br/>
? ? ? ?</span> <span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">return</span></span><span style="color:#000000;">?data;<br/>
? ? });<br/>
});</span></div></div><div><div style="font-size:16px;"><pre style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;word-break:break-all;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;"><span style="color:#008000;"><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;">//</span></span><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;"><span style="color:#008000;">使用factory方法</span></span>
app.factory(<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'remoteData'</span>,<span style="color:#0000ff;">function</span><span style="color:#000000;">(){
    </span><span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">var</span></span> data = {name:<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'n'</span>,<span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">value</span>:<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'v'</span><span style="color:#000000;">};
    </span><span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">return</span></span><span style="color:#000000;"> data;
});</span></pre></div><div style="font-size:16px;"><pre style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;word-break:break-all;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;"><span style="color:#008000;"><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;">//</span></span><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;"><span style="color:#008000;">使用service方法</span></span>
app.service(<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'remoteData'</span>,<span style="color:#0000ff;">function</span><span style="color:#000000;">(){
    </span><span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">this</span></span>.name = <span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'n'</span><span style="color:#000000;">;
    </span><span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">this</span></span>.<span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">value</span> = <span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'v'</span><span style="color:#000000;">;
});</span></pre></div><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">Module的factory和$provide的factory方法是一模一样的，从官网文档看它们其实就是一回事。至于Module内部是如何调用的，我此处并不打算深究，我只要知道怎么用就好了。</span></span></p><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">再看Module的service方法，它没有return任何东西，是因为service方法本身返回一个构造器，系统会自动使用new关键字来创建出一个对象。所以我们看到在构造器函数内可以使用this，这样调用该服务的地方便可以直接通过remoteData.name来访问数据了。</span></span></p><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">下面我们来用一下自己定义好的服务：</span></span></p><h2 style="margin:0px 0px 0.5em;font-family:inherit;color:inherit;text-rendering:optimizeLegibility;font-weight:bold;font-size:18px;text-indent:1em;">三、管理服务的依赖关系</h2><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">服务与服务中间可以有依赖关系，例如我们这里定义一个名为validate的服务，它的作用是验证数据是否合法，它需要依赖我们从远程获取数据的服务remoteData。代码如下：</span></span></p><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">? 在factory的参数中，我们可以直接传入服务remoteData，ng的依赖注入机制便帮我们做好了其他工作。不过一定要保证这个参数的名称与服务名称一致，ng是根据名称来识别的。若参数的名次与服务名称不一致，你就必须显示的声明一下，方式如下：</span></span></p><div style="font-size:16px;"><pre style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;word-break:break-all;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;">
app.factory(<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'validate'</span>,[<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'remoteData'</span>,<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">function</span></span><span style="color:#000000;">(remoteDataService){
    </span><span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">return</span></span> <span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">function</span></span><span style="color:#000000;">(){
        </span><span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">if</span></span>(remoteDataService.name==<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'n'</span><span style="color:#000000;">){
            alert(</span><span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'验证通过'</span><span style="color:#000000;">);
        }
    };
}]);</span></pre></div><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">我们在controller中注入服务也是同样的道理，使用的名称需要与服务名称一致才可以正确注入。否则，你必须使用$inject来手动指定注入的服务。比如：</span></span></p><div style="font-size:16px;"><pre style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;word-break:break-all;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;"><span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">function</span></span><span style="color:#000000;"> <span style="color:rgb(153, 0, 0);font-weight:bold;">testC</span>(scope,rd){</span><span style="color:#000000;">
    scope.getData </span>= <span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">function</span></span><span style="color:#000000;">(){
        alert(</span><span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'name：'</span>+rd.name+<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'   value：'</span>+<span style="color:#000000;">rd.value);
    }
}
testC.$inject </span>= [<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'$scope'</span>,<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">'remoteData'</span>];
</pre></div><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.75em; text-indent: 1em;"><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">ng服务的基本知识也就这些了。目前只是学些皮毛，或许以后用到项目中了才能体会到他的强大之处，以及在真实使用中的这样那样的问题。</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><br/></span></div><div><hr/></div><div><span style="font-size: 19px;">内置服务</span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;">window服务</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 13px; display: block; padding: 9.5px; margin: 0px 0px 10px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 1px solid rgb(204, 204, 204); border-radius: 4px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(245, 245, 245);"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: inherit; padding: 0px; color: inherit; border-radius: 0px; background-color: transparent;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: navy;">&lt;script&gt;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><br/>

inside;"><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Comic Sans MS', 微软雅黑;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 68, 68);">? defer() 创建一个deferred对象，这个对象可以执行几个常用的方法，比如resolve,reject,notify等。使用deferred对象的promise，可以创建Promise对象。</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Comic Sans MS', 微软雅黑;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 68, 68);">??</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Comic Sans MS', 微软雅黑;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 68, 68);">all() 传入Promise对象数组，批量执行，返回一个promise对象</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Comic Sans MS', 微软雅黑;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 68, 68);">??</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Comic Sans MS', 微软雅黑;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 68, 68);">when() 传入一个不确定的参数，如果符合Promise标准，就返回一个promise对象</span></span></span></div></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-size: 13px;"><span style="font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, color="#333333" face="Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, Courier New, monospace" size="2">在Promise中，定义了三种状态：未完成状态、完成状态、拒绝状态。并且状态的变更是不可逆的；未完成状态可以变成完成状态、拒绝状态。使用resolve方法变成完成状态、使用reject方法变成拒绝状态。</font></div><div><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 12px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 12px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: <a name="1152"/>
<h1>AngularJS过滤器</h1>
<div>
<table bgcolor="#D4DDE5" border="0">
<tr><td><b>创建时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-29 17:21</i></td></tr>
<tr><td><b>更新时间：</b></td><td><i>2016-8-30 9:17</i></td></tr>
</table>
</div>
<br/>

<div>
<span><div style="-evernote-webclip:true"><span style="color: inherit;"><span style="font-family: inherit;"><span style="font-size: 24px;">AngularJS的Filter用法详解</span></span></span></div><div style="box-shadow:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0980392) 0px 4px 10px;background:white;box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgb(254, 254, 254);"><div style="padding-bottom: 5px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: dashed; border-bottom-color: rgb(211, 211, 211); font-size: 14px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px;"><div><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="margin-right:5px;"><a href="http://www.tuicool.com/sites/uMvu6vM" style="text-decoration:none;transition:0.25s;outline:none 0px;overflow:hidden;white-space:nowrap;word-break:keep-all;text-overflow:ellipsis;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);display:inline;" target="_blank"></a></span></span></div></div><div><span style="color: rgb(153, 153, 153);"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><i style="font-style:normal;float:left;">原文</i>? <a href="http://www.cnblogs.com/wushangjue/p/4516107.html?utm_source=tuicool&amp;utm_medium=referral" style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);text-decoration:none;transition:0.25s;outline:none 0px;overflow:hidden;white-space:nowrap;word-break:keep-all;text-overflow:ellipsis;max-width:69%;display:inline-block;">http://www.cnblogs.com/wushangjue/p/4516107.html</a></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(153, 153, 153);"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="margin-right:5px;">主题</span> <a href="http://www.tuicool.com/topics/11060094" style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);text-decoration:none;transition:0.25s;outline:none 0px;" target="_blank"><span style="display:inline-block;padding:2px 4px;font-size:0.9em;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:nowrap;color:rgb(120, 120, 120);text-decoration:none;background-color:rgb(242, 242, 242);margin-right:5px;">AngularJS</span></a></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><br/></span></div></div><div style="padding:20px 5px 25px;margin-bottom:0px;overflow-x:hidden;word-wrap:break-word;word-break:break-all;min-height:340px;font-size:16px;"><div style="font-size:16px;"><h2 style="margin:0px 0px 0.5em;font-family:inherit;color:inherit;text-rendering:optimizeLegibility;font-weight:bold;font-size:18px;text-indent:1em;">Filter简介</h2><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">Filter是用来格式化数据用的。</span></span></p><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">Filter的基本原型（ '|' 类似于Linux中的管道模式）：</span></span></p><pre style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;word-break:break-all;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;">
{{ expression | filter }}
</pre><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">Filter可以被链式使用（即连续使用多个filter）：</span></span></p><pre style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;word-break:break-all;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;">
{{ expression | filter1 | filter2 | ... }}
</pre><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">Filter也可以指定多个参数：</span></span></p><pre style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;word-break:break-all;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;">
{{ expression | filter:argument1:argument2:... }}
</pre><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; text-rendering: optimizelegibility; text-indent: 1em; font-size: 18px;"><div><b><span style="color: inherit;"><span style="font-family: inherit;">AngularJS内建的Filter</span></span></b></div></div><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; font-family: inherit; color: inherit; text-rendering: optimizelegibility; font-size: 16px; text-indent: 1em; font-weight: bold;"><div>currency：</div></div><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">用途：格式化货币</span></span></p><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">方法原型：</span></span></p><pre style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;word-break:break-all;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">function</span>(amount, currencySymbol, fractionSize)
</pre><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">用法：</span></span></p><div style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;"><span style="color:#008080;">1</span>?{{?12?|?currency}}? <span style="color:#008000;"><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;">&lt;!--</span></span><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;"><span style="color:#008000;">将12格式化为货币，默认单位符号为?'$',?小数默认2位</span><span style="color:#008000;">--&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#008080;">2</span>?<br/><span style="color:#008080;">3</span>?{{?12.45?|?currency:'￥'}}?<span style="color:#008000;"><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;">&lt;!--</span></span><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;"><span style="color:#008000;">将12.45格式化为货币，使用自定义单位符号为?'￥',?小数默认2位</span><span style="color:#008000;">--&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#008080;">4</span>?<br/><span style="color:#008080;">5</span>?{{?12.45?|?currency:'CHY￥':1}}?<span style="color:#008000;"><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;">&lt;!--</span></span><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;"><span style="color:#008000;">将12.45格式化为货币，使用自定义单位符号为?'CHY￥',?小数指定1位,?会执行四舍五入操作?</span><span style="color:#008000;">--&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#008080;">6</span>?
<div><span style="color:#008080;">7</span>?{{?12.55?|?currency:undefined:0}}?<span style="color:#008000;"><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;">&lt;!--</span></span><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;"><span style="color:#008000;">将12.55格式化为货币，?不改变单位符号，?小数部分将四舍五入?</span><span style="color:#008000;">--&gt;</span></span></div></div><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; font-family: inherit; color: inherit; text-rendering: optimizelegibility; font-size: 16px; text-indent: 1em; font-weight: bold;"><div>date：</div></div><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">用途：格式化日期</span></span></p><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">方法原型：</span></span></p><pre style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;word-break:break-all;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">function</span>(date, format, timezone)
</pre><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">用法：</span></span></p><div style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;"><span style="color:#008000;"><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;">&lt;!--</span></span><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;"><span style="color:#008000;">使用ISO标准日期格式?</span><span style="color:#008000;">--&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#000000;"><br/>
{{?'2015-05-20T03:56:16.887Z'?|?date:&quot;MM/dd/yyyy?@?h:mma&quot;}}<br/><br/></span><span style="color:#008000;"><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;">&lt;!--</span></span><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;"><span style="color:#008000;">使用13位（单位：毫秒）时间戳?</span><span style="color:#008000;">--&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#000000;"><br/>
{{?1432075948123?|?date:&quot;MM/dd/yyyy?@?h:mma&quot;}}<br/><br/></span><span style="color:#008000;"><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;">&lt;!--</span></span><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;"><span style="color:#008000;">指定timezone为UTC?</span><span style="color:#008000;">--&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#000000;"><br/>
{{?1432075948123?|?date:&quot;MM/dd/yyyy?@?h:mma&quot;:&quot;UTC&quot;}}</span></div><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; font-family: inherit; color: inherit; text-rendering: optimizelegibility; font-size: 16px; text-indent: 1em; font-weight: bold;"><div>filter：</div></div><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">用途：过滤数组</span></span></p><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">方法原型：</span></span></p><pre style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;word-break:break-all;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">function</span>(array, expression, comparator)
</pre><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">用法1（参数expression使用String）：</span></span></p><div style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;"><div><span style="color:#008080;">1</span>?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">div</span>?</span><span style="color:#ff0000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 128, 128);">ng-init</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">=<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">&quot;myArr?=?[{name:'Tom',?age:20},?{name:'Tom?Senior',?age:50},?{name:'May',?age:21},?{name:'Jack',?age:20},?{name:'Alice',?age:22}]&quot;</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">2</span>? ? ?<span style="color:#008000;"><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;">&lt;!--</span></span><span style="color:rgb(153, 153, 136);font-style:italic;"><span style="color:#008000;">?参数expression使用String，将全文搜索关键字?'a'?</span><span style="color:#008000;">--&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">3</span>? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">div</span>?</span><span style="color:#ff0000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 128, 128);">ng-repeat</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">=<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">&quot;u?in?myArr?|?filter:'a'?&quot;</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">4</span>? ? ? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">p</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span>Name:{{u.name}}<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;/</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">p</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">5</span>? ? ? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">p</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span>Age:{{u.age}}<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;/</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">p</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">6</span>? ? ? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">br</span>?</span><span style="color:#0000ff;">/&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">7</span>? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;/</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">div</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">8</span>?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;/</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">div</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div></div><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">用法2（参数expression使用function）：</span></span></p><div style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;"><span style="color:#008080;">?1</span>?<span style="color:#000000;">//?先在Controller中定义function:?myFilter<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;">?2</span>?<span style="color:#000000;">$scope.myFilter?=?function?(item)?{<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;">?3</span>?<span style="color:#000000;">? ? return?item.age?===?20;<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;">?4</span>?<span style="color:#000000;">};<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;">?5</span>?
<div><span style="color:#008080;">?6</span>?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">div</span>?</span><span style="color:#ff0000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 128, 128);">ng-repeat</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">=<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">&quot;u?in?myArr?|?filter:myFilter?&quot;</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">?7</span>? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">p</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span>Age:{{u.age}}<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;/</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">p</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">?9</span>? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">br</span>?</span><span style="color:#0000ff;">/&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">?10</span>?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;/</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">div</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div></div><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">用法3（参数expression使用object）：</span></span></p><div style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;"><div><span style="color:#008080;">1</span>?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">div</span>?</span><span style="color:#ff0000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 128, 128);">ng-init</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">=<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">&quot;myArr?=?[{name:'Tom',?age:20},?{name:'Tom?Senior',?age:50},?{name:'May',?age:21},?{name:'Jack',?age:20},?{name:'Alice',?age:22}]&quot;</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">2</span>? ? ? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">p</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span>Name:{{u.name}}<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;/</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">p</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">4</span>? ? ? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">p</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span>Age:{{u.age}}<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;/</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">p</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">5</span>? function(<span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">object</span>, spacing)
</pre><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">用法（将对象格式化成标准的JSON格式）：</span></span></p><div style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;">{{?{name:'Jack',?age:?21}?|?json}}<br/></div><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; font-family: inherit; color: inherit; text-rendering: optimizelegibility; font-size: 16px; text-indent: 1em; font-weight: bold;"><div>limitTo：</div></div><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">方法原型：</span></span></p><pre style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;word-break:break-all;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">function</span>(input, limit)
</pre><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">用法（选取前N个记录）：</span></span></p><div style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;"><div><span style="color:#008080;">1</span>?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">div</span>?</span><span style="color:#ff0000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 128, 128);">ng-init</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">=<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">&quot;myArr?=?[{name:'Tom',?age:20},?{name:'Tom?Senior',?age:50},?{name:'May',?age:21},?{name:'Jack',?age:20},?{name:'Alice',?age:22}]&quot;</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">2</span>? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">div</span>?</span><span style="color:#ff0000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 128, 128);">ng-repeat</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">=<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">&quot;u?in?myArr?|?limitTo:2&quot;</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div><div><span style="color:#008080;">3</span>? ? ? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">p</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#000000;">Name:{{u.name}}</span></div><span style="color:#008080;">4</span>? ? ? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">p</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#000000;">Age:{{u.age}}</span><div><span style="color:#008080;">5</span>? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;/</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">div</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#008080;">6</span>?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;/</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">div</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span></div></div><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; font-family: inherit; color: inherit; text-rendering: optimizelegibility; font-size: 16px; text-indent: 1em; font-weight: bold;"><div>lowercase/uppercase：</div></div><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">方法原型：</span></span></p><pre style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;word-break:break-all;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;">
function(<span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">string</span>)
</pre><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">用法：</span></span></p><div style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;"><span style="color:#000000;">China?has?joined?the?{{?&quot;wto&quot;?|?uppercase?}}.<br/>
We?all?need?{{?&quot;MONEY&quot;?|?lowercase?}}.</span></div><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; font-family: inherit; color: inherit; text-rendering: optimizelegibility; font-size: 16px; text-indent: 1em; font-weight: bold;"><div>number:</div></div><p style="margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:16px;text-indent:1em;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Tahoma, Arial, STXihei, 'Microsoft YaHei', 微软雅黑, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">方法原型：</span></span></p><pre style="padding:0.3em;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-radius:4px;display:block;margin:0px 0px 0.75em;font-size:12px;font-family:Monaco, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace;word-break:break-all;word-wrap:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;border:1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.14902);background-color:rgb(246, 246, 246);overflow-y:auto;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">function</span>(number, fractionSize)

? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ?<span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">if</span></span><span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">?(specified_char?</span><span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">!=</span>?<span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;"><span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">''</span></span>?<span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">&amp;&amp;</span><span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">?input[i]?</span><span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">===</span><span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">?specified_char)?{<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 153, 153);">26</span></span>?<span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? output?</span><span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">+=</span><span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">?input[i].toUpperCase();<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 153, 153);">27</span></span>?<span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? }<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 153, 153);">28</span></span>? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ?<span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">else</span></span><span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">?{<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 153, 153);">29</span></span>?<span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? output?</span><span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">+=</span><span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">?input[i];<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 153, 153);">30</span></span>?<span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? }<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 153, 153);">31</span></span>?<span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? }<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 153, 153);">32</span></span>?<span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? }<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 153, 153);">33</span></span>?<br/><span style="color:#008080;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 153, 153);">34</span></span>? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? ?<span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-weight:bold;">return</span></span><span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">?output;<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 153, 153);">35</span></span>?<span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">? ? ? ? ? ? ? ? };<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 153, 153);">36</span></span>?<span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">? ? ? ? ? ? });<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 153, 153);">37</span></span>?<br/><span style="color:#008080;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 153, 153);">38</span></span>?<span style="background-color:#f5f5f5;color:#000000;">? ? ? ? })();<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 153, 153);">39</span></span>? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;/</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">script</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#008080;">40</span>?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;/</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">head</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#008080;">41</span>?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">body</span>?</span><span style="color:#ff0000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 128, 128);">ng-app</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">=<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">&quot;ngCustomFilterTest&quot;</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#008080;">42</span>? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">input</span>?</span><span style="color:#ff0000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 128, 128);">ng-model</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">=<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">&quot;yourinput&quot;</span></span><span style="color:#ff0000;">?<span style="color:rgb(0, 128, 128);">type</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">=<span style="color:rgb(221, 17, 68);">&quot;text&quot;</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#008080;">43</span>? ? ?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">&lt;</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;"><span style="color:#800000;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">br</span>?</span><span style="color:#0000ff;">/&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#008080;">44</span>?<span style="color:#000000;">? ? Result:?{{?yourinput?|?capitalize_as_you_want:3:'b'?}}<br/></span><span style="color:#008080;">45</span>?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0, 128);font-weight:normal;">body</span></span><span style="color:#0000ff;">&gt;</span></span><span style="color:#008080;">46</span>?<span style="color:#0000ff;"><span style="color:rgb(0, 0,
